SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Date], [t].[Location], [t].[Name], [t0].[Id], [t0].[EventId], [t0].[IsAttending], [t0].[UserId], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[Email], [t0].[Password], [t0].[Role], [t0].[Username]
FROM (
    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Date], [e].[Location], [e].[Name]
    FROM [Events] AS [e]
    ORDER BY [e].[Id]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[EventId], [a].[IsAttending], [a].[UserId], [u].[Id] AS [Id0], [u].[Email], [u].[Password], [u].[Role], [u].[Username]
    FROM [Attendances] AS [a]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [a].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[EventId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t0].[Id]
